<name>MELISSA CEPEDA</name>< Date>
1605580105737<//Date>
<Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
As I faced a puddle of antifreeze in my driveway, I chose this shop because of the reviews although I thought to myself, it might be too good to be true. Luckily I found that Star Auto definitely lives up to the 5 star rating! This shop has figured out how to merge excellent customer service with skilled expertise and I am absolutely impressed. I know the amount of work it takes even to get a decent diagnosis in my compact/Tetris engine, and this shop was able to provide one quickly. They gave me the information I needed to make an informed decision regarding necessary and recommended repairs and services. Best of all, the prices are very reasonable. First time visiting this place. I had a driver's side window that wouldn't roll down so of course I needed to get it fixed before I get pulled over by a cop and they end up shooting me because I refused to roll down my window. I called up a few places, all which sounded shady until I finally called Star Auto Service.

The lady receptionist passed me over to Rob, and Rob was very helpful. He told me to bring in my car to the shop and that his team would help diagnose the problem and let me know once they know what the issue is before charging me for any repairs. After dropping the car off, Rob actually offered to call an Uber/Lyft to take me back to my work so I wouldn't have to walk. That's great service right there! A few hours later he called and confirmed that the rotor and motor were damaged and needed to be replaced. Luckily he was able to do it all in one day so I was able to get my car back by closing time and it was working great.

Unfortunately, the next day the window suddenly failed and again, I reached out to Rob and had him take a look, after his diagnostic, he confirmed that the electrical harness was damaged and explained to me in great detail how it can happen and how to insure that it doesn't happen again, he would use a longer harness.

I got my car back and now everything has been working fine. Normally mechanics are known be shady and give off that vibe, but not with Rob and his team at Star Auto Service. I'm very impressed with the customer service and quality of work. I saw some people complain about the prices but honestly, it's not much different than other shops around the area, at least for me and I'm willing to pay a few extra bucks to get the great service I got here.</review>

<Time>1563232056522< /Time><Rating>2< /Rating><text>I have mixed feelings about my visit so I'll write an honest review. I brought my old car here before for tint and there was bubbles so I knew not to go here for tint again and thought they couldn't possibly mess up a subwoofer. The guys who installed my amp and sub did a great job, especially considering I showed up with a car full of junk on a Friday afternoon. It sounds okay too, after some adjustments. The thing is, I specifically asked for 1000 watts. Half way home after picking up, I knew something was wrong. I had a 500 watt amp and two 250 watt subs instead of the 1000 watts that I repeatedly asked for, but they were closed. The next day the salesman I dealt with insisted that a 500 watt amp and two subs that can handle that 500 watts IS a "1000 watt system". I was shocked because I've installed systems in all my cars and dealt with music equipment for as long as I can remember and this is not a thing. A guitar speaker cabinet and head unit, for example, would be advertised as 200 watts because it is 200 watts of power, not a 100 watt head and four 25 watt speakers. I get that the speakers can handle that divided power, but nobody adds the watts the amp outputs with the watts the speakers can handle and calls it whatever the outcome of that equation happens to be. I called around to other audio shops and nobody does that. The dude played me. If I knew I would be getting half the power I would have done it myself for so much cheaper. He told me it would be 300$ more to upgrade to the system I want and that my old 1000 watt amp was weaker. The ease and straight face with which he told me that I have a "1000 watt system" with a 500 watt amp makes me think this is what he does regularly. I encourage everyone who brought their vehicle here to check exactly what was installed, as some others may not be as electronically inclined and susceptible to being taken advantage of. I also encourage future customers to be thoroughly verbal with the salesman in order to prevent this. Although, I thought I was thorough, considering I specifically asked for 1000 watts many times. Just beware and be aware.< /text><pics>None</pics>< Response>
None<//Response>
